except RuntimeError:  # pragma: no cover\n                raise configexc.ValidationError(\n                    pattern, \"must be a valid regex - recursion depth \"\n                    \"exceeded\")\n\n        assert recorded_warnings is not None\n\n        for w in recorded_warnings:\n            if (issubclass(w.category, DeprecationWarning) and\n                    str(w.message).startswith('bad escape')):\n                raise configexc.ValidationError(\n                    pattern, \"must be a valid regex - \" + str(w.message))\n            else:\n {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01G4wuw2DbWcNrRy7ZJX4ToG","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Perfect! I found the issue. Let me analyze the code:\n\nIn the `_parse_value` method (lines 1004-1018), the code does:\n1. Try to parse as an integer directly\n2. If that fails:\n   - If it ends with '%', strip the '%' and set `mult = 255.0 / 100` (which equals 2.55)\n   - Otherwise, set `mult = 255.0`\n3. Then multiply the parsed float value by `mult`\n\nThe problem is that this `_parse_value` method is used for ALL color channels - both RGB and HSV. For RGB, the range is 0-255, so using `255.0 / 100` as the multiplier for percentages is correct. But for HSV's hue component, the range is 0-359, so percentages should use a different multiplier: `359.0 / 100 = 3.59`.\n\nThe bug is that:\n- When parsing `hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)`, the hue 100% The saturation and value channels (0-255) are correct.\n\nExpected behavior:\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) should parse to (359, 255, 255)\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) should parse to (179, 127, 127) approximately\n- hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%) should parse to (359, 255, 255, 255)\n- hsva(50%, 50%, 50%, 100%) should parse to (179, 127, 127, 255) approximately\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\nfrom qutebrowser.config import configtypes\n\n\nclass TestHSVPercentageParsing:\n    \"\"\"Test HSV percentage parsing bug.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue_is_wrong(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) produces wrong hue (~254 instead of 359).\n\n        This test PASSES on buggy code. It demonstrates the bug by checking\n        that hue is incorrectly set to ~254-255 instead of 359.\n        \"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        # Parse hsv with 100% for all channels\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # On buggy code: hue~254-255 (100% of 255), saturation~254-255, value~254-255\n        # On fixed code: hue=359 (100% of 359), saturation~254-255, value~254-255\n        hue = result.hue()\n        saturation = result.saturation()\n        value = result.value()\n\n        # The bug: hue should be ~359 but is ~254-255\n        assert 250 <= hue <= 255, (\n            f\"Buggy code produces hue around 254-255 when parsing hsv(100%, 100%, 100%), \"\n            f\"but got {hue}\"\n        )\n        # S and V are correct at ~254-255 (100% of 255)\n        assert 250 <= saturation <= 255\n        assert 250 <= value <= 255\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue_is_wrong(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) produces wrong hue (127 instead of ~179).\n\n        This test PASSES on buggy code.
